	Hydra.MusicOverride("Sanctuary_Eastern_Continent", "Music_Scosglen_TurDulra_Hostile")
--	Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtFeet(idActorGizmo, Memory_POI_Power)
--	Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(trans_out_power, "TRANS_OUT", idActorGizmo)
	Hydra.ActorSetConversationList(idActorNPC, "NPC_Conversation_Override_Empty")
	local tWildlife = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("CAMP_TurDulra_Wildlife")
	for i, idActor in pairs(tWildlife) do
		if Hydra.ActorIsAlive(idActor) then
			Hydra.ActorKill(idActor)
		end
	end

	local tDruidVisions = Hydra.ActorsLinkedByActorInGroup(astaroth_vis_loc, "asta_druid")
	local tFireBursts = Hydra.ActorsLinkedByActorInGroup(astaroth_vis_loc, "fireBurstLocs")

	Hydra.Wait(2)
	
	for i, vision in pairs(tDruidVisions) do
		Hydra.QActorFaceActor(vision, astaroth_walk_loc)
		Hydra.ActorSetAnimSetOverride(vision, "NPC_Combat_1HS")
		Hydra.Wait(.2)
	end
	
--	for i, vision in pairs(tIntroVisions) do

--		Hydra.ActorSetCollidable(vision, false)
--	end
	Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(ghost_fadein, "TRANS_IN", astaroth_vision)
	
	Hydra.Wait(2)
	Hydra.ActorPlaySimpleConversation(Intro_Echo, mainIntroDruid)
	Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationConstantSpeed(astaroth_vision, astaroth_walk_loc, Hydra.MOVE_RATE_WALK, false)
	Hydra.Wait(3)
	Hydra.QActorPower(astaroth_vision, "Generic_Taunt")
	Hydra.Wait(3)
	Hydra.QActorPlayEffectGroup(astaroth_vision, "astaroth_boss_tripleAttack_right")
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	Hydra.QActorPower(astaroth_vision, "Generic_NPC_Attack")
	Hydra.Wait(.5)
	Hydra.WeatherOverride("Sanctuary_Eastern_Continent", "weather_scosglen_TurDurla_fire")

	for i, vision in pairs(tDruidVisions) do
		Hydra.QActorPower(vision, "AnimKey_Fall_Backwards")
	end

	for i, vision in pairs(tIntroVisions) do
		Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(trans_out_power, "TRANS_OUT", vision)
	end
	
--	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectSize(mainIntroDruid, 3)
--	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectDuration(mainIntroDruid, 3)
--	for i, loc in pairs(tFireBursts) do
--		Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroupActorToActor(mainIntroDruid, loc, "fxKit_damaging_burstRope_fire")
--	end

	Hydra.ActorPlaySound(idActorPlayer, male_scream)
	Hydra.ActorPlaySound(idActorPlayer, female_scream)
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtFeet(treeLoc, Intro_Memory_POI_Power)
	
	for i, idSpawner in pairs(tSkeletonSpawners) do
		Hydra.ActorGizmoSetDisabled(idSpawner, false)
	end
end

</td></tr><tr><td><b>arLevelAreas</b></td><td><a href="..\LevelArea\Scos_TurDulra.lvl.md">[DT_SNO] LevelArea: "Scos_TurDulra"</a>
</td></tr><tr><td><b>arSubzones</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_6a71535</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSnonameTokens</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_47705e2</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>eIndicatorType</b></td><td><code>2</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_9c1ea4f</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>fDebugDisable</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_b185921</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>dwFlags</b></td><td><code>2</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>dwLinesSeconds</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start(idActorKiller, idActorKilled)
	eastern_elite_killed = true
	
	for i, idActor in pairs(tSkeletonSpawnersEast) do
		Hydra.ActorDisable(idActor)
	end
	
	local tSkeletons = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("CAMP_TurDulra_FireSkeletons_East")
	for i, idActor in pairs(tSkeletons) do
		Hydra.Wait(.2)
		if Hydra.ActorIsAlive(idActor) then
			Hydra.ActorKill(idActor)
		end
	end
	
	Hydra.Wait(1.5)
	Hydra.ActorPlayConversation(Boss_Taunt_Conv, idPlayer)

			Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(meteorLoc, "astaroth_boss_meteorstorm_impact")

		Hydra.ActorPlaySound(idActor, male_scream)
		Hydra.ActorPlaySound(idActor, female_scream)
		Hydra.Wait(.1)
		for i, vision in pairs(tVisions) do
			Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(trans_out_power, "TRANS_OUT", vision)
		end
		for i, meteorLoc in pairs(tMeteorLoc) do
			Hydra.ActorDisable(meteorLoc)
		end
		Hydra.Wait(1)
		Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(trans_out_power, "TRANS_OUT", astarothVision)
		Hydra.ActorTriggerSpawnerUpdateLinkedToActor(idActorDetector)
		Hydra.ActorDisable(idActorDetector)
	end
end
